CVE-2019-0708
(9.8 CRITICAL)

EPSS: 97.50%

1 posts

A remote code execution vulnerability exists in Remote Desktop Services formerly known as Terminal Services when an unauthenticated attacker connects to the target system using RDP and sends specially crafted requests, aka 'Remote Desktop Services Remote Code Execution Vulnerability'.

simontsui at 2023-11-08T14:48:16.592Z **ASEC** summarized 17 months of a Kimsuky operation dubbed _Operation Covert Stalker_. Kimsuky is a nation-state APT attributed to North Korea and assessed to be in the Reconnaissance General Burueau (RGB). In the report (Korean language only) ASEC states that Kimsuky sends phishing emails to targets involved in the field of North Korea, exploiting CVE-2019-0708 (9.8 critical RDP vulnerability allowing for RCE, added to KEV Catalog 03 November 2021) and other unidentified vulnerabilities, adding remote control programs e.g. AnyDesk and Quasar RAT etc., and encrypting systems with BlackBit ransomware. **Link:** [https://asec.ahnlab.com/en/58654/](https://asec.ahnlab.com/en/58654/) [#Kimsuky](https://infosec.exchange/tags/Kimsuky) [#NorthKorea](https://infosec.exchange/tags/NorthKorea) [#APT](https://infosec.exchange/tags/APT) [#cyberespionage](https://infosec.exchange/tags/cyberespionage) [#IOC](https://infosec.exchange/tags/IOC) [#CVE20190708](https://infosec.exchange/tags/CVE20190708) [#Blackbit](https://infosec.exchange/tags/Blackbit) [#ransomware](https://infosec.exchange/tags/ransomware) [#anydesk](https://infosec.exchange/tags/anydesk) [#quasarRAT](https://infosec.exchange/tags/quasarRAT) [#RGB](https://infosec.exchange/tags/RGB)

CVE-2023-22518
(9.8 CRITICAL)

EPSS: 96.76%

30 posts

All versions of Confluence Data Center and Server are affected by this unexploited vulnerability. This Improper Authorization vulnerability allows an unauthenticated attacker to reset Confluence and create a Confluence instance administrator account. Using this account, an attacker can then perform all administrative actions that are available to¬†Confluence instance administrator leading to - but

Walker at 2023-11-09T14:02:04.386Z To help mitigate the [#atlassian](https://infosec.exchange/tags/atlassian) [#confluence](https://infosec.exchange/tags/confluence) [#ransomware](https://infosec.exchange/tags/ransomware) as a result of [#cve202322518](https://infosec.exchange/tags/cve202322518) 1\. Dont run Jira or Confluence as root on the linux box. (Good advice for any web app). 2\. Install the database on a different machine from the web server. Even if your web server gets compromised and encrypted the data in Jira will remain safe and recoverable. 3\. Encrypt the database tables for added protection against data theft. 4\. Keep multiple daily server backups / snapshots so you can recover from a clean backup. 5\. Monitor outbound traffic for spikes realted to data exfiltration. 6\. Monitor CPU for spikes that might represent encryption activity. MOST IMPORTANT - DONT RUN Atlassian products on the open Internet! [#incidentresponse](https://infosec.exchange/tags/incidentresponse)

H3liumb0y at 2023-11-07T08:23:17.021Z Atlassian has raised the severity of CVE-2023-22518 from CVSS 9.1 to üîü, the highest critical rating, due to a change in the attack's scope. This critical security advisory concerns CVE-2023-22518, which highlights an improper authorization vulnerability in Confluence Data Center and Server. The vulnerability, now rated at a CVSS score of üîü, the highest critical rating, enables an unauthenticated attacker to reset Confluence and create an administrator account, potentially leading to a complete data compromise. Atlassian has detected active exploitation and strongly recommends immediate application of the provided fixes. If immediate patching is not possible, temporary mitigations such as network restrictions and specific configuration changes can be implemented. It is imperative for customers to thoroughly review their threat detection systems for any signs of compromise and follow their security incident response plan if any evidence of a breach is discovered. üõ°Ô∏è Source: [https://confluence.atlassian.com/security/cve-2023-22518-improper- authorization-vulnerability-in-confluence-data-center-and- server-1311473907.html](https://confluence.atlassian.com/security/cve-2023-22518-improper- authorization-vulnerability-in-confluence-data-center-and- server-1311473907.html) [#Atlassian](https://infosec.exchange/tags/Atlassian) [#SecurityUpdate](https://infosec.exchange/tags/SecurityUpdate) [#CVE202322518](https://infosec.exchange/tags/CVE202322518)

Walker@infosec.exchange at 2023-11-09T14:02:04.000Z To help mitigate the [#atlassian](https://infosec.exchange/tags/atlassian) [#confluence](https://infosec.exchange/tags/confluence) [#ransomware](https://infosec.exchange/tags/ransomware) as a result of [#cve202322518](https://infosec.exchange/tags/cve202322518) 1\. Dont run Jira or Confluence as root on the linux box. (Good advice for any web app). 2\. Install the database on a different machine from the web server. Even if your web server gets compromised and encrypted the data in Jira will remain safe and recoverable. 3\. Encrypt the database tables for added protection against data theft. 4\. Keep multiple daily server backups / snapshots so you can recover from a clean backup. 5\. Monitor outbound traffic for spikes realted to data exfiltration. 6\. Monitor CPU for spikes that might represent encryption activity. MOST IMPORTANT - DONT RUN Atlassian products on the open Internet! [#incidentresponse](https://infosec.exchange/tags/incidentresponse)

CVE-2023-46604
(9.8 CRITICAL)

EPSS: 96.57%

9 posts

The Java OpenWire protocol marshaller is vulnerable to Remote Code Execution. This vulnerability may allow a remote attacker with network access to either a Java-based OpenWire broker or client to run arbitrary shell commands by manipulating serialized class types in the OpenWire protocol to cause either the client or the broker (respectively) to instantiate any class on the classpath. simontsui at 2023-11-10T12:30:19.506Z **Aon** identified a unique Atlassian Confluence backdoor that persists even after patching CVE-2023-22515. CVE-2023-1671
(9.8 CRITICAL)

EPSS: 94.67%

CVE-2023-38545
(9.8 CRITICAL)

EPSS: 0.07%

1 posts

This flaw makes curl overflow a heap based buffer in the SOCKS5 proxy handshake. When curl is asked to pass along the host name to the SOCKS5 proxy to allow that to resolve the address instead of it getting done by curl itself, the maximum length that host name can be is 255 bytes. If the host name is detected to be longer, curl switches to local name resolving and instead passes on the resolved

CVE-2023-36671
(6.3 MEDIUM)

EPSS: 0.05%

3 posts

An issue was discovered in the Clario VPN client through 5.9.1.1662 for macOS. The VPN client insecurely configures the operating system such that all IP traffic to the VPN server's IP address is sent in plaintext outside the VPN tunnel even if this traffic is not generated by the VPN client. This allows an adversary to trick the victim into sending plaintext traffic to the VPN server's IP address

EPSS: 0.05%

On Windows, The IsLocal function does not correctly detect reserved device names in some cases. alanc@fosstodon.org at 2023-11-17T18:16:03.000Z The 'sxadm status' command in [#OracleSolaris](https://fosstodon.org/tags/OracleSolaris) 11.4.63 has added two new extensions that it reports on. BTC_NO is reported for AMD CPUs that are not susceptible to the Branch Type Confusion vulnerability (CVE-2022-23825). SMEP is reported for Intel & AMD CPUs which have enabled Supervisor Mode Execution Prevention. (SMEP has been enabled since Oracle Solaris 11.1 on Intel's Ivy Bridge and later processors, but was not previously reported by the sxadm command. AMD support came later.)

dangoodin at 2023-11-14T21:35:00.537Z Intel on Tuesday pushed microcode updates to fix a high-severity CPU bug that has the potential to be maliciously exploited against cloud-based hosts. The flaw, affecting virtually all modern Intel CPUs, causes them to ‚Äúenter a glitch state where the normal rules don‚Äôt apply,‚Äù Tavis Ormandy, one of several security researchers inside Google who discovered the bug, reported. Once triggered, the glitch state results in unexpected and potentially serious behavior, most notably system crashes that occur even when untrusted code is executed within a guest account of a virtual machine, which, under most cloud security models, is assumed to be safe from such faults. Escalation of privileges is also a possibility. The bug, tracked under the common name Reptar and the designation CVE-2023-23583, is related to how affected CPUs manage prefixes, which change the behavior of instructions sent by running software. Intel x64 decoding generally allows redundant prefixes‚Äîmeaning those that don‚Äôt make sense in a given context‚Äîto be ignored without consequence. During testing in August, Ormandy noticed that the REX prefix was generating ‚Äúunexpected results‚Äù when running on Intel CPUs that support a newer feature known as fast short repeat move, which was introduced in the Ice Lake architecture to fix microcoding bottlenecks. [https://arstechnica.com/security/2023/11/intel-fixes-high-severity-cpu-bug- that-causes-very-strange- behavior/](https://arstechnica.com/security/2023/11/intel-fixes-high-severity- cpu-bug-that-causes-very-strange-behavior/)

simontsui at 2023-11-13T14:27:44.887Z **Ivanti** security advisory: Two vulnerabilities impact all supported versions of the products ‚Äì EPMM Versions 11.10, 11.9 and 11.8 and Sentry Versions 9.18. 9.17 and 9.16. Older versions/releases are also at risk. * CVE-2023-39335 (vendor 8.5 high severity) - Authenticated User enroll as another user vulnerability * CVE-2023-39337 (vendor 6.8 medium) - Authenticated user obtain certificate for another user vulnerability By taking advantage of a physically stolen device insider threats who already have a valid user certificate, or systems that have open enrollment, a threat actor can impersonate an authenticated user to: Obtain a valid certificate for another EPMM user; Enroll a device for another EPMM user. The vulnerabilities can be chained to allow an unauthenticated user to access resources behind Sentry. Older versions/releases are also at risk. * CVE-2023-39335 (vendor 8.5 high severity) - Authenticated User enroll as another user vulnerability * CVE-2023-39337 (vendor 6.8 medium) - Authenticated user obtain certificate for another user vulnerability By taking advantage of a physically stolen device insider threats who already have a valid user certificate, or systems that have open enrollment, a threat actor can impersonate an authenticated user to: Obtain a valid certificate for another EPMM user; Enroll a device for another EPMM user. The vulnerabilities can be chained to allow an unauthenticated user to access resources behind Sentry. Because of the prerequisite information required for exploitation, the attacker would have to be highly sophisticated to perform the attack chain. **Link:** [https://www.ivanti.com/blog/ivanti-epmm- cve-2023-39335-39337](https://www.ivanti.com/blog/ivanti-epmm- cve-2023-39335-39337) [#Ivanti](https://infosec.exchange/tags/Ivanti) [#EPMM](https://infosec.exchange/tags/EPMM) [#MobileIronCore](https://infosec.exchange/tags/MobileIronCore) [#Vulnerability](https://infosec.exchange/tags/Vulnerability) [#CVE202339335](https://infosec.exchange/tags/CVE202339335) [#CVE202339337](https://infosec.exchange/tags/CVE202339337) [#IvantiSentry](https://infosec.exchange/tags/IvantiSentry)

simontsui at 2023-11-16T15:32:58.084Z [@BleepingComputer](https://infosec.exchange/@BleepingComputer) Fortinet's [security advisory](https://www.fortiguard.com/psirt/FG-IR-23-135) gives a different CVSSv3 score compared to what they as the CNA provided [NIST and NVD](https://nvd.nist.gov/vuln/detail/CVE-2023-36553). CVE-2023-46835
(0 None)

EPSS: 0.00%

2 posts

N/A

simontsui at 2023-11-15T16:22:51.937Z **Citrix** is fashionably late to Patch Tuesday. Their security advisory is for Citrix Hypervisor: * CVE-2023-23583 (CVSS: 8.8 high severity) This issue may allow unprivileged code in a guest VM to compromise that VM and, potentially, the host. CVE-2023-23583 only affects systems running on Intel Ice Lake or later CPUs. * CVE-2023-46835 (unknown CVSS score) An issue has been discovered that affects Citrix Hypervisor 8.2 CU1 LTSR and may allow malicious privileged code in a guest VM to compromise an AMD-based host via a passed through PCI device. CVE-2023-46835 only affects systems that have both of i) a PCI device passed through to the guest VM by the host administrator and also ii) an AMD CPU. **Link:** [https://support.citrix.com/article/CTX583037/citrix-hypervisor- security-bulletin-for-cve202323583-and- cve202346835](https://support.citrix.com/article/CTX583037/citrix-hypervisor- security-bulletin-for-cve202323583-and-cve202346835) [#Citrix](https://infosec.exchange/tags/Citrix) [#CitrixHypervisor](https://infosec.exchange/tags/CitrixHypervisor) [#vulnerability](https://infosec.exchange/tags/vulnerability) [#PatchTuesday](https://infosec.exchange/tags/PatchTuesday) [#CVE202323583](https://infosec.exchange/tags/CVE202323583) [#CVE202346835](https://infosec.exchange/tags/CVE202346835)
